              <div class="widget Blog" id="Blog1">
               <div class="blog-posts hfeed">
                <!-- google_ad_section_start(name=default) -->
                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Tuesday, August 28, 2012
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry">
                    <a name="3398173809573671477">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                     Dragon Gate, Kota Damansara: Small Morsels of Traditional Yum Cha Snacks
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-3398173809573671477">
                     <br/>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-h-odl_VpJmY/UDu69_29ocI/AAAAAAAAMvU/4i2ODypvnY8/s1600/DSC_0138.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-h-odl_VpJmY/UDu69_29ocI/AAAAAAAAMvU/4i2ODypvnY8/s640/DSC_0138.JPG" width="492" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                       <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                        <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                         Yum Cha Affair at a Dragons Lair!
                         <o:p>
                         </o:p>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </b>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        No dragons found here but then again I am sure the mythical creature would not be missed here! Our usual foodies rounded up one weekend morning and met up for a yum cha session at
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Dragon Gate Restaurant
                        </b>
                        at Kota Damansara. A boldly named restaurant, Dragon Gate has only been around less than a year.
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-B84Jw10WL9E/UDu6rPHaddI/AAAAAAAAMsE/QD2aysj-b8o/s1600/DSC_0004.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="424" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-B84Jw10WL9E/UDu6rPHaddI/AAAAAAAAMsE/QD2aysj-b8o/s640/DSC_0004.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        Boasting a local chef who learned the art of Dim Sum from a Hong Kong Dim Sum chef,
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Dragon Gate Restaurant
                        </b>
                        offers quite a list of dim sum variety with lots of classics and a few creative newbies. The ambience at the restaurant is really bright and quite spacious with lots of natural lights and coolness. Al fresco area is also available if one insisted on dining ala naturel. Huge posters of dim sum are strategically placed all over the restaurant to make one salivate at its offerings!
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-z3sCDx7nypo/UDu6-sjYy7I/AAAAAAAAMvc/BdKRrMLvbdU/s1600/Dragon+Gate+Ambience.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-z3sCDx7nypo/UDu6-sjYy7I/AAAAAAAAMvc/BdKRrMLvbdU/s1600/Dragon+Gate+Ambience.jpg" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-3xc-LOaAhhg/UDu68sIob9I/AAAAAAAAMvE/AvUMq3D8CT8/s1600/DSC_1012.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="424" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-3xc-LOaAhhg/UDu68sIob9I/AAAAAAAAMvE/AvUMq3D8CT8/s640/DSC_1012.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        A long bar parallel to the dining area offers customer a peek at the operation of the restaurant while stacks of baskets are seen stacked neatly in one corner to remind one of the nature of the restaurant. Marble table tops are displayed with essential utensils and sauces for self service. I could see lots of wait staff scurrying around busy as a bee! A hot warmer display is laden with loads of fried goodies, beckoning everyone entering the restaurant to head over to check out the samples.
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Zc9ItsPgxkk/UDu6r0xeogI/AAAAAAAAMsM/O6-2u_r0OEM/s1600/DSC_0008.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Zc9ItsPgxkk/UDu6r0xeogI/AAAAAAAAMsM/O6-2u_r0OEM/s640/DSC_0008.JPG" width="424" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-PEpIFPld1P4/UDu69Ab5sZI/AAAAAAAAMvM/tFNMpdup5As/s1600/DSC_1023.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="424" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-PEpIFPld1P4/UDu69Ab5sZI/AAAAAAAAMvM/tFNMpdup5As/s640/DSC_1023.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        One interesting point at Dragon Gate is that they also serve a minimal list of beverages like Ice Coffee or Tea, Herbal Drinks, and Tong Shui in addition to the usual Chinese Tea. I just couldnt resist and ordered an Iced Tea. My
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Iced Tea
                        </b>
                        was quite lovely as it had a fairly thick and creamy concoction of refreshing tea. It tasted so good that I finished this in a jiffy!
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        Others had herbal beverages like chilled
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Sea Coconut with Longan
                        </b>
                        and
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Sugarcane with Water Chestnut
                        </b>
                        . I also tried the Sea Coconut and thought it was decent.
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                       <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                        <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                         The Steamy Collection
                         <o:p>
                         </o:p>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </b>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/---J4bLmwGJw/UDu614aj_WI/AAAAAAAAMt8/Wi2xVN3gkJI/s1600/DSC_0080.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="424" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/---J4bLmwGJw/UDu614aj_WI/AAAAAAAAMt8/Wi2xVN3gkJI/s640/DSC_0080.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-CiViBYV-ZWc/UDu6zmDyvpI/AAAAAAAAMtk/9e1cdJTAIkM/s1600/DSC_0058.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-CiViBYV-ZWc/UDu6zmDyvpI/AAAAAAAAMtk/9e1cdJTAIkM/s640/DSC_0058.JPG" width="424" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        In every dim sum meal, my two ultimate favorites will always be
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Siew Mai
                        </b>
                        and
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Har Kow
                        </b>
                        . In anticipation of the two classics, the Siew Mai was only mediocre while the Har Kow fared better. I simply prefer my Siew Mai to exude more bouncy texture with a great savory taste. The one here was smooth in texture and flavor was average, lending the overall to be not as par to my usual benchmark for the classic dumpling. Har Kow or Shrimp Dumpling fared better with a good thin translucent skin encasing a fresh amount of shrimp filling. Lovely in flavors with a hint of natural sweetness from the shrimp, the Har Kow was snatched quickly by the gang.
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-j5zF3dmkN2w/UDu66aSuanI/AAAAAAAAMus/d-wgL2_AzB4/s1600/DSC_0175.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-j5zF3dmkN2w/UDu66aSuanI/AAAAAAAAMus/d-wgL2_AzB4/s640/DSC_0175.JPG" width="424" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                       <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                        <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                         Siew Mai with Salted Egg
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                        wasdecent but not particularly memorable. A bit more rustic compared to the classic Siew Mai, this one had light hint of the glorious salted egg yolk. Maybe more salted egg would perk up this one!
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-eOcFUbuMcF4/UDu6snkOzOI/AAAAAAAAMsU/IKonT1cc17I/s1600/DSC_0013.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-eOcFUbuMcF4/UDu6snkOzOI/AAAAAAAAMsU/IKonT1cc17I/s640/DSC_0013.JPG" width="424" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        While the classic fell short, others were good on its own merit! Leading the scrumptious lot of the dim sum was
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Bacon Rolls with Honey Sauce
                        </b>
                        , featuring three superb rolls of lardy delight. Strip of bacon delicately wrapped around a minced fish and prawn filling and bathe in a sweet honey sauce is the ultimate morsels of flavors at Dragon Gate. I also like how the bacon retains a subtle dense texture against the smooth filling of the seafood paste while the contrasting taste of salty bacon balanced out the sweet honey beautifully. Highly recommended on my books!
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">

                     </div>

                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-IaPiJ7zdGN0/UDu6utLplnI/AAAAAAAAMss/yW8_5sJe6Ds/s1600/DSC_0024.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-IaPiJ7zdGN0/UDu6utLplnI/AAAAAAAAMss/yW8_5sJe6Ds/s640/DSC_0024.JPG" width="424" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                       <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                        <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                         Shanghai Xiao Long Bao
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                        is considerably good here at Dragon Gate. Yes, certainly not at par with other Xiao Long Bao specialist but for a dim sum restaurant, it fared good in terms of the thin skin engulfing a broth of meaty filling. I didnt count the essential 18 folds of the soupy dumpling but it passed with a degree of goodness wink!
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">

                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-W4d71sj4Dps/UDu6vz5p2jI/AAAAAAAAMs8/DVQLokvXiCI/s1600/DSC_0035.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-W4d71sj4Dps/UDu6vz5p2jI/AAAAAAAAMs8/DVQLokvXiCI/s640/DSC_0035.JPG" width="424" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                       <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                        <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                         Cabbage Dumpling
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                        is simply adorable at sight. A bundle of sweet flavors from the hints of vegetable and shrimp filling, this one fared pretty good in texture, flavors and presentation.
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qjr4jbGGHoo/UDu64uqwsII/AAAAAAAAMuc/CQmxQGArpi0/s1600/DSC_0155.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="424" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qjr4jbGGHoo/UDu64uqwsII/AAAAAAAAMuc/CQmxQGArpi0/s640/DSC_0155.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        My partner is a huge fan of
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Steamed Fish Ball
                        </b>
                        so he regards himself as a connoisseur of the dim sum. This one rated decent for him but again far away from his own benchmark of fish balls. I stole a small bite and thought it was decent. There is a light bouncy texture and portion wise was deemed large compared to others I had before.
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-QBM5F3FuELY/UDu7C_4NNnI/AAAAAAAAMwM/LAFKhy7CFRI/s1600/Blog10.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-QBM5F3FuELY/UDu7C_4NNnI/AAAAAAAAMwM/LAFKhy7CFRI/s1600/Blog10.jpg" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                       <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                        <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                         Superior Soup Dumplings
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                        and
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Seafood Dumpling Soup
                        </b>
                        both features stuffed Sui Kow served in a light golden broth. Both dumplings may look the same but tasted differently due to the stuffing and size. The regular Sui Kow had again a fine minced filling while the large Seafood Dumpling was stuffed to the brim with a variety of minced seafood. For the price tag it came with, I certainly have no complaints on either dumplings.
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                       <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                        <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                         Dumplings with Superior Soy Sauce
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                        also featured the similar Sui Kow but this time soaked in a superior soy sauce and sprinkled with fried shallots and sesame seed. An aromatic one, the dumplings had the distinctive taste of the lovely soy sauce and shallot flavors, lifting up the flavors another notch compared to the earlier Sui Kow.
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-pbtbTXCaLeg/UDu62lYi4AI/AAAAAAAAMuE/epFTYTRn6WM/s1600/DSC_0088.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-pbtbTXCaLeg/UDu62lYi4AI/AAAAAAAAMuE/epFTYTRn6WM/s640/DSC_0088.JPG" width="424" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                       <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                        <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                         Steamed Pork Ribs
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                        was so delicious, we had to order two more! Executed perfectly, the pieces of meaty ribs were tender, moist and pumped up with a moreish flavor. I adored the meat tremendously laced with lots of umami flavors and a hint of black bean. It was unanimous that we could not get enough of this dim sum!
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">

                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">

                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-2-p1is-okXY/UDu65QDi8uI/AAAAAAAAMug/ZvUzbM9kq-U/s640/DSC_0162.JPG" width="424" yda="true"/>
                      </a>

                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">

                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        Not a fan of chicken feet, I only heard positive feedbacks on
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Stewed Chicken Feet
                        </b>
                        from others. From appearance, it did look really appetizing and chicken feet lovers did praised its portion of nicely stewed tender chicken feet.

                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">

                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">

                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-YfsxJNZILd4/UDu9G8Am8iI/AAAAAAAAMwY/vOoF_ThZxKA/s1600/DSC_0153.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="424" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-YfsxJNZILd4/UDu9G8Am8iI/AAAAAAAAMwY/vOoF_ThZxKA/s640/DSC_0153.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        Not a usual dish found in every dim sum outlet, I have to commend Dragon Gate for the
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Herbal Chicken
                        </b>
                        . A large basket held a foil packet of herbal steamed chicken guaranteed to entice ones nostril upon the opening of the packet. Pieces of tender chook had a good boost of herb flavors while retaining its moist and sweetness. The chef is very generous with the amount of herbs hence the dish is really praiseworthy for those who love a good herbal soup concoction. I did savor spoonful of the rich herb broth happily!
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                       <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                        <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                         Hot Steamed Buns
                         <o:p>
                         </o:p>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </b>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-0ykNBJWOIj4/UDu7CEFIpII/AAAAAAAAMwE/1Te66rxWv6E/s1600/Blog9.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-0ykNBJWOIj4/UDu7CEFIpII/AAAAAAAAMwE/1Te66rxWv6E/s1600/Blog9.jpg" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        Limited choices of baos but sufficient to say, it has the few must-haves in any dim sum restaurant. Six choices ranging from classic
                        <strong>
                         Char Siew Bao, Lotus Paste, Red Bean, Pandan Kaya
                        </strong>
                        to newbies
                        <strong>
                         Black Sesame
                        </strong>
                        and
                        <strong>
                         Custard &amp; Salted Egg Yolk
                        </strong>
                        . Char Siew Bao was indeed fluffy that day and filled with the typical Char Siew Filling. I preferred the Black Sesame Bun for its texture and aroma compared to the Custard &amp; Salted Egg Yolk.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <o:p>
                        <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        </span>
                       </o:p>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                       <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                        <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                         The Fry Up Collection
                         <o:p>
                         </o:p>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </b>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-aUgHPApdIzI/UDu6tBrlRuI/AAAAAAAAMsc/ZEFE_HlOX-Y/s1600/DSC_0015.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-aUgHPApdIzI/UDu6tBrlRuI/AAAAAAAAMsc/ZEFE_HlOX-Y/s640/DSC_0015.JPG" width="424" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        I could never resist deep fried goodies, can you? Although not considered a healthy option of dim sum, still one should always leave a little room for some indulgence in small portions. In addition, if a good fry up is executed with fresh batches of oil and good heat, the dish is not as bad as it is deemed (heard about this in a food documentary television episode recently).
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-CMZfqszIYwc/UDu6wug7m0I/AAAAAAAAMtE/uzkOOd6PDf0/s1600/DSC_0041.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="424" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-CMZfqszIYwc/UDu6wug7m0I/AAAAAAAAMtE/uzkOOd6PDf0/s640/DSC_0041.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                       <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                        <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                         Sweet Potato &amp; Yam
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                        proved to be a delicious creation! Ordinary looking but filled ones mouth with a lovely contrasting texture of crispy breaded shell filled with a creamy and silky filling of sweet potato and powdery yam. Well executed without a trace of oil, these little golden balls also got everyones nod of approval for its simplicity in flavors and textures. I would order this again for a revisit.
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Tkp-0RDgdSY/UDu60aujd-I/AAAAAAAAMts/R0Fqn1RPyAw/s1600/DSC_0064.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Tkp-0RDgdSY/UDu60aujd-I/AAAAAAAAMts/R0Fqn1RPyAw/s640/DSC_0064.JPG" width="424" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        My favorite fried dim sum, when done perfectly, was
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Radish Cake
                        </b>
                        . Dragon Gate Radish Cake had high scores from me for its perfect crisp exterior and moist tender interior. I thought the flavors were spot on with a good taste of white radish. Well-fried, the radish cake was not oily at all but rather crisp and melt-in-the-mouth goodness all the way. Yum!!
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-pyMLnCs1c-E/UDu61Pi_wZI/AAAAAAAAMt0/aZgTt833vwA/s1600/DSC_0073.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-pyMLnCs1c-E/UDu61Pi_wZI/AAAAAAAAMt0/aZgTt833vwA/s640/DSC_0073.JPG" width="424" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        Essentially sumptuous was the
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Crispy Yam Puff
                        </b>
                        , balls of crispy yam filled with sweet bbq pork filling. Scoring high points, the yam puff was fluffy and crispy with a creamy taste. Go ahead order this to check it out for yourself.
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-aEKfKjzZhnw/UDu7BWex21I/AAAAAAAAMv8/nPHEbuXHtrQ/s1600/BBQ+Pies.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-aEKfKjzZhnw/UDu7BWex21I/AAAAAAAAMv8/nPHEbuXHtrQ/s1600/BBQ+Pies.jpg" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        I didnt manage to sample any
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         BBQ Pies
                        </b>
                        . It was only when it was finished, everyone raved about how lovely this one was. I did manage to capture how the layers of flaky pastry looked with the savory and sweet filling. Ok, I will take their word for it for this flaky pastry roll filled with BBQ meat filling and rounded up with pork floss.
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                      <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-NS7qGFqeTF4/UDu7DYNyvNI/AAAAAAAAMwQ/X21DXurpv8w/s1600/Blog11.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                       <img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-NS7qGFqeTF4/UDu7DYNyvNI/AAAAAAAAMwQ/X21DXurpv8w/s1600/Blog11.jpg" yda="true"/>
                      </a>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                       <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                        <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                         Beancurd Rolls with Shrimp
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                        had a repeat in orders when we found out how delicious it was. Light, crispy and filled with juicy sweet shrimp filling, its best eaten hot with a dab of mayonnaise. I had mine with mustard and chili sauce that was quite sensational despite its simplicity.
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Wasabi Shrimp Ball
                        </b>
                        is the inherited touch of Japanese cuisine that made its way into our Chinese one. Its the wasabi sauce with that tingling sensation at the back of the nose that makes this dim sum appealing. Other than that said, the shrimp ball was ordinary. Between the both, I seemed to prefer the lighter Beancurd Rolls with Shrimp.
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <o:p>
                        <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        </span>
                       </o:p>
                      </span>
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <o:p>
                        <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        </span>
                       </o:p>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                       <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                        I thought
                        <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                         Shrimp Rolls with Mango
                        </b>
                        was a great combination! The sweet mango lightens up the sweet shrimp paste while the crispy texture was delicious against the soft and subtle filling. I do agree with another foodies comment that they should put a bit more mango in the roll for a stronger hint of fruitiness or even a sweet Thai chili sauce for a boost of flavors. Other than that said, its a nice dim sum for a variety touch.
                        <o:p>
                        </o:p>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <br/>
                     </div>
                     <div align="center" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: normal; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; text-align: center;">
                      <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                       <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                        <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                         Crispy Flour Rolls with Mayo
                        </span>
                       </b>
                       <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                        is fried You Tiao stuffed with shrimp paste and doused with liberally mayonnaise. I couldnt taste much shrimp filling and thought the mayonnaise overkilled the dim sum. Sometimes less is more, so less mayonnaise and maybe a bit more shrimp paste in this one would up this dim sum several notches.
                        <span style="font-family: 'Verdana','sans-serif';">
                         <span style="font-family: Verdana, sans-serif;">
                          Pan fried
                          <b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">
                           Shanghai Guo Tie
                          </b>
                          also faired mediocre at best. Plump and pan seared nicely, the fried dumpling was decent.
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                     </div>
                     <o:p>
                     </o:p>

                       <img border="0" height="424" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Yr5wlzqqXVM/UDu6t9dKbrI/AAAAAAAAMsk/XQ8RJi6mT68/s640/DSC_0019.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
